    <link rel="canonical" href="https://patents.google.com/patent/US20230356923A1/en">
    <meta name="description" content="
     Exemplary embodiments pertain to a combined shipping and expansion device for shipping a roll of unexpanded slit sheet material and for expanding the slit sheet material. In some examples, the device includes: a container made with recyclable paper or board; a roll of slit sheet material wound around a core member and positioned within the container; the roll of slit sheet material having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion; the core member being made with recyclable paper or board and having a length greater than a width of the roll of slit sheet wound around the core member and having protrusions that extend beyond each side of the roll of slit sheet material; a plurality of yoke members within the container, including at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a first of the protrusions and at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a second of the protrusions; and the container having a dispensing opening through which the slit sheet material wound around the core member can be extended and pulled, causing the core member to rotate relative to the yoke members via rotation of the roll of slit sheet material. The combined shipping and expansion device is made from substantially entirely recyclable paper or board materials, whereby after complete dispensing of the slit sheet material from the shipping and expansion device, the combined shipping and expansion device can be recycled in a paper recycling facility. 
   
   ">
    <meta name="DC.type" content="patent">
    <meta name="DC.title" content="Shipping and Dispensing Box for Slit Sheet Material 
       ">
    <meta name="DC.date" content="2023-01-25" scheme="dateSubmitted">
    <meta name="DC.description" content="
     Exemplary embodiments pertain to a combined shipping and expansion device for shipping a roll of unexpanded slit sheet material and for expanding the slit sheet material. In some examples, the device includes: a container made with recyclable paper or board; a roll of slit sheet material wound around a core member and positioned within the container; the roll of slit sheet material having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion; the core member being made with recyclable paper or board and having a length greater than a width of the roll of slit sheet wound around the core member and having protrusions that extend beyond each side of the roll of slit sheet material; a plurality of yoke members within the container, including at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a first of the protrusions and at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a second of the protrusions; and the container having a dispensing opening through which the slit sheet material wound around the core member can be extended and pulled, causing the core member to rotate relative to the yoke members via rotation of the roll of slit sheet material. The combined shipping and expansion device is made from substantially entirely recyclable paper or board materials, whereby after complete dispensing of the slit sheet material from the shipping and expansion device, the combined shipping and expansion device can be recycled in a paper recycling facility. 
   
   ">

            <section>
                <h2>Definitions</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li itemprop="definitions" itemscope repeat>
                        <span itemprop="subject">the preferred embodiments</span>
                        <span itemprop="definition">relate to, e.g., the use of a corrugated box and tensioning device made from paper able to be completely recycled when discarded.</span>
                        <meta itemprop="num_attr" content="0002">
                    </li>
                    <li itemprop="definitions" itemscope repeat>
                        <span itemprop="subject">Each device</span>
                        <span itemprop="definition">has plastics or metals or wood to provide the tensioning required to simultaneously feed and expand the expandable slit sheet material.</span>
                        <meta itemprop="num_attr" content="0003">
                    </li>
                    <li itemprop="definitions" itemscope repeat>
                        <span itemprop="subject">the preferred embodiments</span>
                        <span itemprop="definition">advantageously overcome shortcomings of the above and other background art.</span>
                        <meta itemprop="num_attr" content="0004">
                    </li>

                        <span itemprop="subject">the tension required</span>
                        <span itemprop="definition">is significantly decreased and the strength of the paper is increased. Both benefit the person wrapping by making the tensioning required much less precise, even to the point at which a single tension setting can be used with little or no adjustment. If the tension is set higher than necessary, the increase in strength from the extensible paper keeps the product from tearing and, therefore, makes it easier for the packer to use. Therefore, the packer can make fewer adjustments as the slit sheet roll becomes smaller and smaller (i.e., as the paper is unwound from the roll, reducing the diameter of the remaining paper on the roll).</span>
                        <meta itemprop="num_attr" content="0068">
                    </li>
                    <li itemprop="definitions" itemscope repeat>
                        <span itemprop="subject">a shipping box (“box”) and tensioning device</span>
                        <span itemprop="definition">is made from paper and, most preferably, made from corrugated paper.</span>
                        <meta itemprop="num_attr" content="0069">
                    </li>

            <section itemprop="abstract" itemscope>
                <h2>Abstract</h2>

                <div itemprop="content" html>
                    <abstract mxw-id="PA642534344" lang="EN" source="national office" load-source="docdb">
                        <div class="abstract">Exemplary embodiments pertain to a combined shipping and expansion device for shipping a roll of unexpanded slit sheet material and for expanding the slit sheet material. In some examples, the device includes: a container made
                            with recyclable paper or board; a roll of slit sheet material wound around a core member and positioned within the container; the roll of slit sheet material having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion; the core
                            member being made with recyclable paper or board and having a length greater than a width of the roll of slit sheet wound around the core member and having protrusions that extend beyond each side of the roll of slit sheet
                            material; a plurality of yoke members within the container, including at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a first of the protrusions and at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a second of the protrusions;
                            and the container having a dispensing opening through which the slit sheet material wound around the core member can be extended and pulled, causing the core member to rotate relative to the yoke members via rotation of the
                            roll of slit sheet material. The combined shipping and expansion device is made from substantially entirely recyclable paper or board materials, whereby after complete dispensing of the slit sheet material from the shipping
                            and expansion device, the combined shipping and expansion device can be recycled in a paper recycling facility.</div>
                    </abstract>
                </div>
            </section>

            <section itemprop="description" itemscope>
                <h2>Description</h2>

                <div itemprop="content" html>
                    <ul mxw-id="PDES438083834" lang="EN" load-source="patent-office" class="description">

                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0001]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0002" num="0001" class="description-line">The present application is a continuation of U.S. Ser. No. 16/740,666, filed Jan. 13, 2020, which application is a continuation of U.S. Ser. No. 16/159,186, filed Oct. 12, 2018, now U.S. Pat. No. 10,766,690, of inventor David
                                Goodrich, which is a non-provisional of prior U.S. provisional application No. 62/571,382, filed Oct. 12, 2017 and prior U.S. provisional application No. 62/633,630, file Feb. 22, 2018, the entire disclosures of which four
                                prior applications are all incorporated herein by reference.</div>


                        </li>
                        <heading id="h-0001">BACKGROUND</heading>
                        <heading id="h-0002">Technical Field</heading>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0002]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0003" num="0002" class="description-line">The preferred embodiments relate to, e.g., the use of a corrugated box and tensioning device made from paper able to be completely recycled when discarded.</div>
                        </li>
                        <heading id="h-0003">The Background Art</heading>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0003]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0004" num="0003" class="description-line">There have been a number of devices to dispense expanded slit sheet material. Each device has plastics or metals or wood to provide the tensioning required to simultaneously feed and expand the expandable slit sheet material.</div>
                        </li>
                        <heading id="h-0004">SUMMARY</heading>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0004]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0005" num="0004" class="description-line">The preferred embodiments advantageously overcome shortcomings of the above and other background art.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0005]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0006" num="0005" class="description-line">In accordance with some embodiments of the invention, the use of a shipping box and tensioning device, made completely of paper, enables them both to be completely recycled when the expanded slit sheet material has been fully
                                dispensed.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0006]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0007" num="0006" class="description-line">According to some embodiments of the invention, a combined shipping and expansion device for shipping a roll of unexpanded slit sheet material and for expanding the slit sheet material is provided that includes: a) a container
                                having: a first pair of side wall members; a second pair of side wall members; a bottom panel; and a top cover panel; b) a roll of slit sheet material wound around a core member and positioned within the container; c) the
                                roll of slit sheet material having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion; d) the core member having a length greater than a width of the roll of slit sheet wound around the core member and having protrusions
                                that extend beyond each side of the roll of slit sheet material; e) a plurality of yoke members within the container, including at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a first of the protrusions and at least one
                                yoke member that rotatably receives a second of the protrusions; and f) a friction member arranged to apply frictional pressure against at least one of the protrusions for regulating force required to rotate the roll with
                                respect to the yoke members during unwinding of the roll of slit sheet material from the core member.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0007]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0008" num="0007" class="description-line">In some examples, the core member is a hollow paper tube and the container is formed from corrugated board. In some examples, the yoke members each have an arcuate opening with a radius of curvature that is substantially equal
                                to a radius of the core member. In some examples, the at least one yoke member that rotatably receives the first of the protrusions and the at least one yoke member that rotatably receives the second of the protrusions
                                each include two adjacent yoke members for increased support of each of the protrusions.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0008]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0009" num="0008" class="description-line">In some examples, the adjacent yoke members are separate yoke panels that are placed adjacent one another, with a first of the adjacent yoke panels folded downward over a second of the adjacent yoke panels. In some examples,
                                the first of the adjacent yoke panels includes an extension tab that is received within a receiving slot formed in or proximate the bottom panel, locking the first of the adjacent yoke panels folded downward over the second
                                of the adjacent yoke panels.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0009]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0010" num="0009" class="description-line">In some examples, each of the yoke members being formed on respective contiguous panels connected to the first pair of panels, each of the contiguous panels including a respective one of the arcuate openings, and each of the
                                contiguous panels being folded to a position overlying a respective panel of the first pair of panels such that its respective the arcuate opening is arranged to receive a respective one of the protrusions of the core member.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0010]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0011" num="0010" class="description-line">In some examples, the roll of slit sheet material is positioning within the combined shipping and expansion device and with each of the cylinder protrusions in contact with a respective one of the arcuate openings. In some
                                examples, a first of the second pair of side wall members has an elongated tear-away region extending from a position proximate a first of the second pair of side wall members to a position proximate a second of the second
                                pair of side wall members.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0011]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0012" num="0011" class="description-line">In some examples, the top cover panel being movably mounted above the roll of slit sheet material within the container and being movable to apply pressure to the friction member, and releasable affixing means for releasably
                                affixing the top cover panel with respect to the friction member to regulate the force required to rotate the roll with respect to the yoke members during unwinding of the roll of slit sheet material from the core member.
                                In some examples, the releasable affixing means includes a releasable attachment mechanism that includes at least a portion substantially directly above the core. In some examples, the releasable affixing means includes
                                two releasable attachment mechanisms located proximate opposite sides of the container.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0012]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0013" num="0012" class="description-line">In some examples, the friction member is a tensioning panel having an arcuate surface configured to be pressed against an upper surface of the core. In some examples, the tensioning panel has a through-hole opening that receives
                                one of the protrusions of the core, and wherein the through-hole opening completely surrounds a perimeter of the core such as to be retained by the core. In some examples, the tensioning panel has an elongated slot that
                                extends through a side edge of the tensioning panel such that the tensioning panel is laterally slidable with respect to a protrusion of the core with the protrusion received within the elongated slot. In some examples,
                                the releasable affixing means is a releasable adhesive, and, in some examples, the releasable affixing means is hook and loop fasteners. In some examples, the friction member arranged to apply frictional pressure against
                                at least one of the protrusions includes a tensioning member configured to slidingly move within the container, the tensioning member having an arcuate surface configured to be positioned against the at least one of the
                                protrusions for applying pressure against the at least one of the protrusions. In some examples, the top cover panel is variably movable against a pressing surface of the tensioning member that is opposite to the arcuate
                                surface, whereby the top cover can be moved to increase a force against the pressing surface and increase the pressure applied by the arcuate surface against the at least one of the protrusions.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0013]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0014" num="0013" class="description-line">In some examples, the top cover panel has at least one depending tab member positioned to contact the pressing surface of the tensioning member when the top cover panel is in a closed position. In some examples, the tensioning
                                device having a height that is less than an interior height of the container such that the tensioning device applies pressure to the at least one of the protrusions without contacting the bottom panel. In some examples,
                                the invention further includes at least one removable spacer, the at least one removable spacer being positioned between ends of the roll of slit material and the first pair of panels of the container to stabilize the roll
                                of slit material during shipping of the combined shipping and expansion device. In some examples, the at least one removable spacer includes an elongated slot that extends from an open first end to an arcuate shaped end,
                                thereby forming an elongated channel having an arcuate end, the arcuate end being positioned around the at least one of the protrusions. In some examples, the at least one spacer includes a packing member having downwardly
                                extending panels placed at each end of the roll. In some examples, the at least one spacer includes two spacers, with a respective one of the spacers placed at each end of the roll.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0014]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0015" num="0014" class="description-line">In some examples, the slit sheet paper is extensible and has an extensible range from 1-9% in a machine direction and 1-5% in a cross direction. In some examples, the extensible paper has an extensible range from 1-6% in the
                                machine direction and 1-4% in the cross direction. In some examples, the extensible paper has an extensible range from 1-4% in the machine direction and 1-3% in the cross direction. In some examples, the slit sheet is expandable
                                by applying an expansion force in a range from 0.15 to 0.22 pounds per inch, to form at least one expanded sheet having an array of hexagonal cells. In some examples, the slit sheet paper is a paper having a weight in a
                                range from about 30 to 40 pounds per 3,000 square feet.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0015]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0016" num="0015" class="description-line">According to some other embodiments, a combined shipping and expansion device for shipping a roll of unexpanded slit sheet material and for expanding the slit sheet material is provided that includes: a) a container made with
                                recyclable paper or board; b) a roll of slit sheet material wound around a core member and positioned within the container; c) the roll of slit sheet material having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion;
                                d) the core member being made with recyclable paper or board and having a length greater than a width of the roll of slit sheet wound around the core member and having protrusions that extend beyond each side of the roll
                                of slit sheet material; e) a plurality of yoke members within the container, including at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a first of the protrusions and at least one yoke member that rotatably receives a second
                                of the protrusions; and f) the container having a dispensing opening through which the slit sheet material wound around the core member can be extended and pulled, causing the core member to rotate relative to the yoke
                                members via rotation of the roll of slit sheet material; wherein the combined shipping and expansion device is made from substantially entirely recyclable paper or board materials, whereby after complete dispensing of the
                                slit sheet material from the shipping and expansion device, the combined shipping and expansion device can be recycled in a paper recycling facility.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0016]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0017" num="0016" class="description-line">According to some further embodiments, a method of using the combined shipping and expansion device according to the present invention includes: a) shipping the combined shipping and expansion device to a location of a user;
                                and b) at the location of the user, manually pulling the slit sheet material outward through the dispensing opening and expanding the slit sheet material.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0017]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0018" num="0017" class="description-line">In some examples, the method further includes after fully dispensing the slit sheet material from the container delivering the combined shipping and expansion device to a paper recycling facility. In some examples, the method
                                further includes after fully dispensing the slit sheet material from the container disposing of the combined shipping and expansion device, whereby the combined shipping and expansion device is used as a single-use shipping
                                and expansion device. In some examples, the method further includes that the disposing of the combined shipping and expansion device includes delivering the combined shipping and expansion device to a paper recycling facility
                                for recycling. In some examples, the method further includes providing the container with an elongated tear-away region that covers the dispensing opening during the shipping, and further including removing the tear-away
                                region prior to the manually pulling and expanding.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0018]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0019" num="0018" class="description-line">In some examples, the method further includes applying pressure on the core member during the manually pulling and expanding with a tensioning device that frictionally contacts at least one of the protrusions of the core member.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0019]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0020" num="0019" class="description-line">In some examples, the method further includes adjustably increasing pressure upon the core member via the tensioning device by adjustably positioning of an adjustable panel of the container.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0020]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0021" num="0020" class="description-line">In some examples, the adjustable panel of the container is a cover of the container and adjustably positioning the cover using a releasable affixing means.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0021]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0022" num="0021" class="description-line">In some examples, the method further includes stabilizing the roll of slit material during the shipping with respect to the core member with at least one spacer located proximate opposite ends of the roll of slit material,
                                and removing the at least one spacer prior to the manually pulling and expanding.</div>
                        </li>

                        <heading id="h-0006">DETAILED DESCRIPTION OF THE PREFERRED EMBODIMENTS</heading>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0040]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0041" num="0040" class="description-line">While the present invention may be embodied in many different forms, the illustrative embodiments are described herein with the understanding that the present disclosure is to be considered as providing examples of the principles
                                of the invention and that such examples are not intended to limit the invention to preferred embodiments described herein and/or illustrated herein.</div>
                        </li>
                        <heading id="h-0007">Definitions</heading>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0041]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0042" num="0041" class="description-line">In this application, the following terminology should be interpreted based on the definitions set forth below.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0042]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0043" num="0042" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “Hexacomb” (employed in light of the product trademark Hexacomb®) means a panel constructed of two paper sheet housing vertical hexagonal cells that can be manufactured
                                in various thicknesses to fill gaps.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0043]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0044" num="0043" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the descriptions and terminology in relation to the paper and slit patterns within the embodiments set forth in U.S. Pat. No. 5,667,871, are applicable to some preferred embodiments
                                in this present application.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0044]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0045" num="0044" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “telescope” means a lateral movement of a roll of paper along an axis of the core member, including minimal lateral movement at the region of the roll having the smallest
                                diameter (i.e., closer to the core member) and larger lateral movement at the region of the roll having the largest diameter (i.e., further from the core member). The tendency to telescope is due, in part, to the unexpanded
                                slit sheet paper having a narrower width than the paper core around which the slit sheet paper is wound.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0045]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0046" num="0045" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “paper core” means a round paper tube around which an expanded slit sheet paper is wound.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0046]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0047" num="0046" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “cylinder” as employed herein, means an elongated member or tube having a solid or hollow circular cross-section.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0047]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0048" num="0047" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “contiguous” means that two parts are connected in a continuing sequence, such as, e.g., by a solid or perforated fold line.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0048]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0049" num="0048" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “expandable” as applied to paper sheets, means a paper having a slit pattern that enables the paper to be expanded by opening of the slits upon applying a force in a longitudinal
                                direction of the paper sheet.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0049]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0050" num="0049" class="description-line">Further information relating to the paper, slit patterns, and the expansion process which can be used in some embodiments of the present invention is found in: a) the following U.S. Pat. Nos. 5,538,778; 5,667,871; 5,688,578;
                                5,782,735; 3,908,071; 3,104,197; 3,220,116; 3,266,972; 3,269,393; 3,908,071; 6,024,832; 6,458,447; and 6,712,930; b) the following international PCT application(s): WO 1984002936A1; and c) the following U.S. published applications:
                                2014/901977; 2002/0060034; and 2007/0240841, the entire disclosures of which patents and applications are all incorporated by reference herein, as though recited herein in full.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0050]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0051" num="0050" class="description-line">In addition, the entire disclosures of U.S. Publication 2018/0127197-A1 (U.S. application Ser. No. 15/820,514), U.S. Publication 2018/0222665 A1 (U.S. application Ser. No. 15/428,144) and U.S. Provisional Application 62/524,905
                                (filed as U.S. Non-Provisional application Ser. No. 16/018,702, and internationally published as PCT/US2018/039416) are incorporated by reference herein in their entireties as if recited herein in full as part of the description
                                of the present invention.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0051]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0052" num="0051" class="description-line">Application PCT/US2018/039416 describes a use of extensible paper to greatly reduce the tension required to stretch the slit sheet material. It is particularly useful for the new art shipping box and tensioning device of this
                                application to utilize the extensible paper of the PCT/US2018/039416 application in some preferred embodiments. Although such extensible paper is employed in some preferred embodiments, as described herein other papers
                                can be employed in other embodiments.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0052]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0053" num="0052" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present application, the term “extensible” as applied to paper sheets means a paper sheet that is able to stretch in a longitudinal direction of the paper sheet upon applying a force In the longitudinal
                                direction of the paper sheet. Illustrative extensible sheets are disclosed in U.S. Pat. No. 3,908,071, U.S. patent application Ser. No. 14/901,977 (U.S. Pat. No. 9,945,077), International Application No. WO 1984002936,
                                U.S. Publication Nos. 2002/0060034, 2007/0240841 (U.S. Pat. No. 7,918,966), and U.S. Pat. Nos. 3,104,197, 3,220,116, 3,266,972, 3,269,393, 3,908,071, 6,024,832, 6,458,447, and 6,712,930, the entire disclosures of which
                                are incorporated by reference herein, as though recited herein in full. It should be understood that the stretching of an extensible paper must be measured in an unslit sheet of paper. As disclosed in U.S. Pat. No. 3,266,972,
                                the test and characterization procedures employed in measuring elongation (extensibility) properties can be in accordance with standard TAPPI test Elongation T457. In addition, as disclosed in U.S. Pat. No. 3,266,972, the
                                expression “extensible papers” means a paper having an increasable elongation in the machine direction as compared to standard, non-extensible Kraft paper.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0053]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0054" num="0053" class="description-line">For the purposes of the present invention the term “extensible slit sheet paper” means a paper that is both extensible and expandable. In accordance with another embodiment of the invention, the use of extensible paper reduces
                                the tendency of the slit paper to tear during the expanding of the expandable slit sheet paper without negating the ability to tear the expanded slit sheet paper from the roll of expandable slit sheet paper at the end of
                                the wrapping step.</div>
                        </li>
                        <heading id="h-0008">DETAILED DESCRIPTION</heading>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0054]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0055" num="0054" class="description-line">In accordance with some preferred embodiments of the invention, an expanded slit sheet paper is employed that is made with an extensible paper that, e.g., advantageously substantially reduces a pulling force necessary to expand
                                the expanded slit sheet material. Among other benefits, this reduced pulling force leads to a variety of very substantial benefits, including that it avoids previously required complex resistant devices that were previously
                                necessary and opens the market to smaller manual expansion devices that can be made to be almost completely recyclable,</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0055]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0056" num="0055" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments, machine direction extensibility ranges of the extendible slit sheet paper can have ranges of:
                            </div>
                        </li>
                        <ul>
                            <li id="ul0001-0001" num="0000">
                                <ul>
                                    <li id="ul0002-0001" num="0056">a) from 1.5%-9%, or more preferably from 1.5% to 6%, or even more preferably from 1.5% to 4%; or</li>
                                    <li id="ul0002-0002" num="0057">b) from 2%-9%, or more preferably from 2% to 6%, or even more preferably from 2% to 4%; or</li>
                                    <li id="ul0002-0003" num="0058">c) from 3%-9%, or more preferably from 3% to 6%, or even more preferably from 3% to 4%.</li>
                                </ul>
                            </li>
                        </ul>

                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0059]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0057" num="0059" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments of the present invention, the extensible paper that is employed has low extensible properties as compared to other types of extensible papers. In this regard, an optimal extensible paper enables
                                a smooth transition from an unexpanded to the expanded slit sheet by providing a small amount of stretching at the very start of expansion of the extensible slit sheet paper material.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0060]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0058" num="0060" class="description-line">In accordance with a broad embodiment of the invention, the use of extensible paper reduces the pulling force necessary to stretch the expanded slit sheet material and thereby expands the market to include, e.g., void fill
                                usage and lighter weight papers for greater cushioning effect for very fragile items.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0061]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0059" num="0061" class="description-line">In accordance with another embodiment of the present invention, an extensible slit sheet paper product is produced having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion of the paper product. In some preferred embodiments,
                                the paper product is an extensible paper having an extensibility in the range from 1-9% in the machine direction and 1-5% in the cross direction. Preferably, the extensible paper has an extensible range from 1-6% in the
                                machine direction and 1-4% in the cross direction. Most preferably, the extensible paper has an extensible range from 1-4% in the machine direction and 1-3% in the cross direction.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0062]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0060" num="0062" class="description-line">In accordance with some preferred embodiments of the present invention, an extensible slit sheet paper product is produced having a slit pattern that forms open cells upon expansion of said paper product, wherein said slit
                                sheet is expandable by applying an expansion force in the range from 0.15 to 0.22 pounds per inch, to form at least one expanded sheet having an array of hexagonal cells and where the extensible paper has an extensible
                                range from 1-6% in the machine direction and 1-4% in the cross direction.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0063]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0061" num="0063" class="description-line">For the purposes of expanding the slit sheet paper for use as a packaging wrap, it has been found that cross direction extensible ranges from 1%-5% provides an adequate extensibility, with ranges of 1% to 4% being more preferred,
                                and with ranges of 1% to 3% being most highly preferred.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0064]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0062" num="0064" class="description-line">In some alternative embodiments, cross direction extensibility ranges of the extendible slit sheet paper can have ranges of:
                            </div>
                        </li>
                        <ul>
                            <li id="ul0003-0001" num="0000">
                                <ul>
                                    <li id="ul0004-0001" num="0065">a) from 1.5%-5%, or more preferably from 1.5% to 4%, or even more preferably from 1.5% to 3%; or</li>
                                    <li id="ul0004-0002" num="0066">b) from 2%-5%, or more preferably from 2% to 4%, or even more preferably from 2% to 3%.</li>
                                </ul>
                            </li>
                        </ul>

                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0067]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0063" num="0067" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments, a shipping box with an integrated dispenser is provided. In preferred embodiments, a shipping box with such an integrated dispenser has particular utility and advantages when combined with an
                                extensible paper because of, e.g., the ease of expansion of the extensible paper. Among other things, this can expand the market to customers that use a very small amount of wrap as compared to the industrial market.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0068]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0064" num="0068" class="description-line">Additionally, employment of extensible paper in preferred embodiments also enhances the ease of use by the packer by providing for less ripping during the wrapping process that occurs when the tension is not properly set. As
                                the roll of expanded slit sheet becomes smaller and lighter, there is an increased requirement to increase the tension. With the use of the extensible paper, the tension required is significantly decreased and the strength
                                of the paper is increased. Both benefit the person wrapping by making the tensioning required much less precise, even to the point at which a single tension setting can be used with little or no adjustment. If the tension
                                is set higher than necessary, the increase in strength from the extensible paper keeps the product from tearing and, therefore, makes it easier for the packer to use. Therefore, the packer can make fewer adjustments as
                                the slit sheet roll becomes smaller and smaller (i.e., as the paper is unwound from the roll, reducing the diameter of the remaining paper on the roll).</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0069]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0065" num="0069" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments, a shipping box (“box”) and tensioning device is made from paper and, most preferably, made from corrugated paper.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0070]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0066" num="0070" class="description-line">In the preferred embodiments, the shipping box is also the dispenser/expander of the slit sheet material with tensioning adjustments made using the top flap in combination with two hook and loop strips that hold the tension
                                adjustment in place that presses on the tensioning devices.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0071]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0067" num="0071" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments, a method by which a shipping box is prepared to be used includes the following steps:
                            </div>
                        </li>
                        <ul>
                            <li id="ul0005-0001" num="0000">
                                <ul>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0001" num="0072">(1) The
                                        <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>7</b> </figref> is opened and spacers <b>601</b> and double-sided adhesive strips <b>603</b>, as found in
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref>, are removed.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0002" num="0073">(2) Tensioning devices are placed between
                                        <figure-callout id="106" label="yokes" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">yokes</figure-callout> <b>106</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>1</b> </figref> and slit
                                        <figure-callout id="402" label="paper roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">paper roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>4</b> </figref>, on both sides.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0003" num="0074">(3) Double-sided adhesive strips <b>801</b> are attached to the bottom of the shipping box as shown in
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>8</b> </figref>.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0004" num="0075">(4) Tear-
                                        <figure-callout id="110" label="away strip" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">away strip</figure-callout> <b>110</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIGS. <b>1</b> and <b>2</b> </figref> is removed from the
                                        <figure-callout id="101" label="front panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00007.png" state="{{state}}">front panel</figure-callout> <b>101</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>1</b> </figref>.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0005" num="0076">(5) Expanded
                                        <figure-callout id="602" label="slit sheet material" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet material</figure-callout> <b>602</b> shown in
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref> (i.e., which is optionally used as a protective padding around at least a portion of the
                                        <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                            state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> during shipping) is removed. In some examples, it is removed from under the open
                                        <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png"
                                            state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b>. In some embodiments, it can be removed by unwinding the
                                        <figure-callout id="402" label="slit sheet roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                            state="{{state}}">slit sheet roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> shown in
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>5</b> </figref> and feeding the expanded
                                        <figure-callout id="602" label="slit sheet material" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet material</figure-callout> <b>602</b> through the tear-away
                                        <figure-callout id="110" label="opening" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">opening</figure-callout> <b>110</b> shown in
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>2</b> </figref> until the expanded
                                        <figure-callout id="602" label="material" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">material</figure-callout> <b>602</b> shown in
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref> is fully exits the
                                        <figure-callout id="110" label="opening" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">opening</figure-callout> <b>110</b> and is clear and the
                                        <figure-callout id="404" label="unexpanded slit sheet" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">unexpanded slit sheet</figure-callout> <b>404</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>5</b> </figref> appears.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0006" num="0077">(6) The
                                        <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIGS. <b>5</b> and <b>6</b> </figref> can then be gently closed for the expansion of the full roll of
                                        <figure-callout id="404" label="slit sheet material" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                            state="{{state}}">slit sheet material</figure-callout> <b>404</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIGS. <b>4</b> and <b>5</b> </figref> that requires no tension.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0007" num="0078">(7) As the
                                        <figure-callout id="402" label="slit sheet roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>4</b> </figref> becomes smaller, tension will eventually be required and is done so by closing the
                                        <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png"
                                            state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>2</b> </figref> more firmly in a downward manor and using the hook and loop strips <b>112</b> and <b>113</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>2</b> </figref> to maintain the
                                        <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b> position.</li>
                                    <li id="ul0006-0008" num="0079">(8) As more tension is required the
                                        <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>2</b> </figref> would be adjusted further downward by un-attaching the hook and loop strips <b>112</b> and <b>113</b> of
                                        <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>2</b> </figref> and reattaching them in the new optimum position.</li>
                                </ul>
                            </li>
                        </ul>

                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0080]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0068" num="0080" class="description-line">While the use of hook and loop strips is preferred, in other embodiments, other forms of releasable attachment mechanisms can be employed. For example, in some embodiments, a releasable adhesive can be employed, wherein an
                                adhesively attached closure can be repeatedly opened and resealed. In some examples, a number of appropriate release coatings may be used in some embodiments of the present invention. In some examples, resealable closures
                                can employ features as shown in the following references, which are all incorporated herein by reference in their entireties: G.B. 2147564A; U.S. Pat. No. 2,822,290 (Webber); U.S. Pat. No. 2,880,862 (Sermattei); U.S. Pat.
                                No. 2,985,554 (Dickard); U.S. Pat. No. 4,902,141A (Linnewiel); and U.S. Pub. No. 2002/0164477 (Lonc, et al.).</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0081]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0069" num="0081" class="description-line">Other exemplary resealable closures that can be employed in embodiments of the present invention are shown in the U.S. patents discussed below in this paragraph, the entire disclosures of which are incorporated herein by reference.
                                A first example is shown in U.S. Pat. No. 6,726,054 which is designed for containing breath films or other oral care strips in which the package includes a blister pack having a hinged flap which is resealable against the
                                top surface of the blister pack. The package has a top surface which forms a flange around the perimeter opening of the tray compartment. A second example is shown in U.S. Pat. No. 6,691,886 which includes a plastic tray
                                with a lid film that includes a sealing area around its perimeter which seals to a flange surface of the tray. A third example is shown in U.S. Pat. No. 5,647,506 which shows another resealable container that includes a
                                dispenser for moisture-impregnated articles such as moist tissues using a rigid plastic container with an opening formed in its top surface, wherein a resealable label reseals the top opening.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0082]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0070" num="0082" class="description-line">In preferred embodiments, the hook and loop strips do not interfere with the recyclability of the paper. In some preferred embodiments, the tensioning devices are shipped loose on top of the roll of slit paper within the package
                                and are put in place by the user at the required time—that is, the user preferably installs the tensioning devices when the dispensing is to be commenced.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0083]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0071" num="0083" class="description-line">In some embodiments, when first dispensing the slit sheet paper roll, no tension is necessary. That is, in some embodiments, the initial weight of the roll achieves sufficient frictional resistance to enable expansion of the
                                paper upon pulling by a user without providing additional tension. However, as the roll reduces in weight and diameter during use, the roll will spin more freely due to the decreased weight and require an increasing amount
                                of tension. Thus, in preferred embodiments, a tensioning device is provided.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0084]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0072" num="0084" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments, the shipping box, tensioning device and the paper core upon which the slit sheet material was wound are recyclable, such that, after use, they can be together discarded by placing in a recycling
                                bin or the like for recycling paper.</div>
                        </li>
                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0085]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0073" num="0085" class="description-line">In some preferred embodiments, based on the various diameters and weight weights of the slit sheet roll size, the corrugated material can be single or double wall walled material. In some preferred embodiments, the shipping
                                box and tensioning device are made from single wall material. In some embodiments, the two
                                <figure-callout id="106" label="yokes" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">yokes</figure-callout> <b>106</b> of
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>1</b> </figref> that support the
                                <figure-callout id="403" label="paper core" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">paper core</figure-callout> <b>403</b> of
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>4</b> </figref>, that enables the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="slit sheet roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> of
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>4</b> </figref> to rotate, are also be made with single wall material; for example, such a single wall material can be employed in embodiments having an 8-inch diameter paper roll that weighs 10 pounds. On the other
                                hand, in some embodiments having a 10-inch diameter 20-pound roll, double wall walled corrugated yokes can be employed.</div>
                        </li>

                                    <figure-callout id="108" label="interlocking panels" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">interlocking panels</figure-callout>
                                </figure-callout> <b>107</b> and <b>108</b> with spacer section <b>111</b> (i.e., between the
                                <figure-callout id="105" label="side" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">side</figure-callout> <b>105</b> and yoke <b>106</b>) resting on top. Then, the same process is performed on the right-hand side. The
                                <figure-callout id="116" label="folding flap" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">folding flap</figure-callout> <b>116</b> is then folded inward (e.g., 90 degrees) in relation to the
                                <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b>. In this manner, the hook and
                                <figure-callout id="112" label="loop pads" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">
                                    <figure-callout id="113" label="loop pads" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">loop pads</figure-callout>
                                </figure-callout> <b>112</b> and <b>113</b>, respectively, can now be positioned to make contact and connect together when
                                <figure-callout id="104" label="top flap" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">top flap</figure-callout> <b>104</b> is folded downward and
                                <figure-callout id="116" label="top folding panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">top folding panel</figure-callout> <b>116</b> is pressed towards and against the
                                <figure-callout id="102" label="front panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">front panel</figure-callout> <b>102</b>.
                                <figure-callout id="105" label="Side panels" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">Side panels</figure-callout> <b>105</b> have an
                                <figure-callout id="119" label="additional relief area" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">additional relief area</figure-callout> <b>119</b> that enables
                                <figure-callout id="109" label="top cover tabs" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">top cover tabs</figure-callout> <b>109</b> which, have been folded completely inward, and which are adhered to an underside of the
                                <figure-callout id="104" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>104</b>, to apply pressure to the
                                <figure-callout id="300" label="tensioning devices" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">tensioning devices</figure-callout> <b>300</b> as shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>3</b> </figref> without interference from
                                <figure-callout id="105" label="side panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png" state="{{state}}">side panel</figure-callout> <b>105</b>. In this manner, when the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="slit sheet roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> becomes smaller as it is used (i.e., as paper is dispensed from the roll <b>402</b>), the
                                <figure-callout id="300" label="tensioning device" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">tensioning device</figure-callout> <b>300</b> is pressed downwards to apply a pressure against the
                                <figure-callout id="403" label="core" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">core</figure-callout> <b>403</b> to increase resistance in order to compensate for the smaller (i.e., lighter) slit
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="sheet roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">sheet roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b>, as it is being used up. In the configuration shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>2</b> </figref>, the tear-
                                <figure-callout id="110" label="away flap" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">away flap</figure-callout> <b>110</b> is still in its shipping configuration and is still attached to
                                <figure-callout id="102" label="front panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00002.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">front panel</figure-callout> <b>102</b>.</div>

                                    state="{{state}}">core member</figure-callout> <b>403</b>. That is, the amount of frictional resistance can be adjusted by adjusting the amount of downward pressure that is applied against the tensioning device.</div>

                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0092]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0080" num="0092" class="description-line">With reference to
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref>,
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref> shows an illustrative assembly process for preparing the
                                <figure-callout id="100" label="shipping box" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">shipping box</figure-callout> <b>100</b> for shipping. As shown, a
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> of expanded slit sheet material is wrapped around a core (not shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref>) with the slit sheet material in the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> in an unexpanded state. As shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref>, in order to help further protect the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> during shipping, in some preferred embodiments, a
                                <figure-callout id="602" label="padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> is inserted within the container during shipping. In some embodiments, the
                                <figure-callout id="602" label="padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> can be formed of expanded slit sheet material in an expanded state, and in some embodiments, the
                                <figure-callout id="602" label="padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> can be formed of a plurality of layers of such expanded slit sheet material in such expanded state. In the illustrated example, the
                                <figure-callout id="602" label="padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> is formed so as to surround the roll and can have a substantially rectangular shape that is bent around the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> as shown. In some embodiments, the padding is sized to substantially entirely surround the circumference of the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b>. In some embodiments, the
                                <figure-callout id="602" label="padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> can surround only a portion of the roll, such as, e.g., an upper surface of the roll. Moreover, in some embodiments, the padding can include a plurality of padding portions, with, e.g.,
                                a first padding portion over an upper portion of the roll (e.g., as shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref>) and, e.g., a second padding portion under a lower portion of the roll. In the illustrated example, ends of the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> are exposed below the padding. The padding is preferably employed to help fill any gaps around the periphery of the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> and the walls of the container. As shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>6</b> </figref>, the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> is also preferably sized to substantially fill the container, while the
                                <figure-callout id="602" label="padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> helps fill remaining gaps around the
                                <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> and the four sides of the
                                <figure-callout id="100" label="shipping box" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">shipping box</figure-callout> <b>100</b>. In addition, in the preferred embodiments, thick spacers <b>601</b> are preferably provided to fill spaces at the ends of the roll corresponding to the extended portions of the
                                <figure-callout id="403" label="core" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">core</figure-callout> <b>403</b> extending from the roll. In the preferred embodiments, the spacers are made from multiple layers of corrugated paper or Hexacomb® or the like and are placed adjacent to the
                                <figure-callout
                                    id="402" label="slit sheet roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> and straddling the
                                    <figure-callout id="403" label="core" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">core</figure-callout> <b>403</b> in order to prevent telescoping movement of the
                                    <figure-callout id="402" label="roll" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">roll</figure-callout> <b>402</b> with respect to the
                                    <figure-callout id="403" label="core" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">core</figure-callout> <b>403</b> during shipment. In some preferred embodiments, the spacers <b>601</b> are made one quarter of an inch shorter than the
                                    <figure-callout id="300" label="tensioning device" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                        state="{{state}}">tensioning device</figure-callout> <b>300</b> so that the
                                    <figure-callout id="109" label="folding tabs" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00001.png" state="{{state}}">folding tabs</figure-callout> <b>109</b> do not make contact during shipment. In preferred embodiments, tensioning
                                    <figure-callout id="300" label="devices" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png"
                                        state="{{state}}">devices</figure-callout> <b>300</b> can be placed on top of the expanded slit sheet material or the
                                    <figure-callout id="602" label="like padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00005.png" state="{{state}}">like padding</figure-callout> <b>602</b> for storage during shipment, such as schematically depicted in

As shown, the core protrudes from the

                                </figure-callout> <b>1407</b> and <b>1406</b> as shown in

                        <li>
                            <para-num num="[0101]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0089" num="0101" class="description-line">The assembly of the shipping and dispensing box shown in

                                <figure-callout id="1442" label="side panels" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00013.png" state="{{state}}">side panels</figure-callout> <b>1442</b> of the

                            <para-num num="[0102]"> </para-num>
                            <div id="p-0090" num="0102" class="description-line">In some preferred implementations, the
                                <figure-callout id="1300" label="pressure yolk" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00014.png" state="{{state}}">pressure yolk</figure-callout> <b>1300</b> shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>15</b> </figref> has an oblong shaped opening, preferably an elongated oval shape as shown in
                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>15</b> </figref>. At least the
                                <figure-callout id="1304" label="edge" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00014.png" state="{{state}}">edge</figure-callout> <b>1304</b> of the oblong <b>1302</b> that contacts the core and applies pressure thereto is preferably arcuate, and preferably has an arcuate shape corresponding to the shape of the
                                <figure-callout
                                    id="403" label="core" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">core</figure-callout> <b>403</b>. The opposing
                                    <figure-callout id="1306" label="end" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00014.png" state="{{state}}">end</figure-callout> <b>1306</b> of the oblong can also be arcuate but can any desired configuration since it is not in contact with the core <b>403</b> during the dispensing operation. The closed configuration of the
                                    <figure-callout id="1302" label="oblong opening" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00014.png" state="{{state}}">oblong opening</figure-callout> <b>1302</b> of the

                                    <figure-callout id="1300" label="tensioning yoke" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00014.png" state="{{state}}">tensioning yoke</figure-callout> <b>1300</b> from accidentally being removed from the shipping box when the
                                    <figure-callout id="1402" label="corrugated shipping padding" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00013.png"

                                <figure-callout id="402" label="slit sheet paper" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00000.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png" state="{{state}}">slit sheet paper</figure-callout> <b>402</b>, variable pressure can be applied to the
