                                <figref idrefs="DRAWINGS">FIG. <b>14</b> </figref>, the releasable attachment system is preferably a hook and loop system such as sold under the trademark VELCRO™. In some examples, a strip of
                                <figure-callout id="1412" label="hook fabric" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00013.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">hook fabric</figure-callout> <b>1412</b> is attached at one end to the top <b>1404</b> and a strip of
                                <figure-callout id="1408" label="loop fabric" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">loop fabric</figure-callout> <b>1408</b> is attached to the
                                <figure-callout id="1416" label="side panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">side panel</figure-callout> <b>1416</b>. It should be understood that this arrangement can be reversed, as for example, the
                                <figure-callout id="1412" label="strip" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00013.png"
                                    state="{{state}}">strip</figure-callout> <b>1412</b> can be attached to the
                                <figure-callout id="1416" label="side panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">side panel</figure-callout> <b>1416</b>, and the
                                <figure-callout id="1408" label="strip" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">strip</figure-callout> <b>1408</b> can be attached to the
                                <figure-callout id="1404" label="top cover" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00011.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">top cover</figure-callout> <b>1404</b>. Either <b>1408</b> or <b>1412</b> can be a hook member and the loop member can be on the other of <b>1408</b> or <b>1412</b>. Most preferably, the attachment system is positioned
                                so that pressure is applied directly above the
                                <figure-callout id="403" label="core member" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00003.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png" state="{{state}}">core member</figure-callout> <b>403</b>. Towards that end, in the illustrated embodiment, it is, thus, most preferable that the downward pressure on the
                                <figure-callout id="1300" label="tensioning panel" filenames="US20230356923A1-20231109-D00012.png,US20230356923A1-20231109-D00014.png"

For example, in some embodiments, when the box is supported on a horizontal surface, in some embodiments, the releasable attachment system is at least partly located vertically
                                above a region within a diameter of the core (i.e., such as to be directly above at least a portion of the core), and, in some preferred embodiments, the releasable attachment system includes at least a portion directly
                                above substantially the central axis of the core.</div>

                                member having a surface configured to be positioned against said at least one of said protrusions for applying pressure against said at least one of said protrusions.</div>

                                and increase the pressure applied against said at least one of said protrusions.</div>

        if (window.help && window.help.service) {
            helpApi = window.help.service.Lazy.create(0, {
                apiKey: 'AIzaSyDTEI_0tLX4varJ7bwK8aT-eOI5qr3BmyI',
                locale: 'en-US'
            });
            window.requestedSurveys = new Set();
            window.requestSurvey = function(triggerId) {
                if (window.requestedSurveys.has(triggerId)) {
                    return;
                }
                window.requestedSurveys.add(triggerId);
                helpApi.requestSurvey({
                    triggerId: triggerId,
                    enableTestingMode: false,
                    callback: (requestSurveyCallbackParam) => {
                        if (!requestSurveyCallbackParam.surveyData) {
                            return;
                        }
                        helpApi.presentSurvey({
                            productData: {
                                productVersion: window.version,
                                customData: {
                                    "experiments": "",
                                },
                            },
                            surveyData: requestSurveyCallbackParam.surveyData,
                            colorScheme: 1,
                            customZIndex: 10000,
                        });
                    }
                });
            };

            window.requestSurvey('YXTwAsvoW0kedxbuTdH0RArc9VhT');
        }
